pgd_ctrp=pyqsbvat_ctrp
verif_phiy_cind=(1.0-((phiy_cind_sind+phiy_cind_strp+phiy_cind_sser+phiy_cind_senj)))*100.0
t2_mat_co2_senj=elem_r2_mat_co2_senj_2015*ems_mat_co2_senj
pcid_ctrp_sser=pyqsbvat_ctrp+t2val_ci_ctrp_sser/ci_ctrp_sser
verif_all2=0.0
ems_ch_hfc=(ems_ch_hfc_cenj)
bal_trade_val_cenj=px_cenj*x_cenj-pm_cenj*m_cenj
pxm_cind=pmsbvat_cind
subst_f_l_sind=adjust6_f_l_sind*subst_f_n_l_sind+(1.0-adjust6_f_l_sind)*lag(subst_f_l_sind,-1)
subst_f_mat_sind=adjust6_f_mat_sind*subst_f_n_mat_sind+(1.0-adjust6_f_mat_sind)*lag(subst_f_mat_sind,-1)

gr_prog_k_sind=gr_prog_exo_k_sind
